    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem exploration-step21)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen backyard living-room pantry driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at backyard)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored backyard)
    (explored living-room)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen backyard north)
    (door-open kitchen backyard north)
    (door-between backyard kitchen south)
    (door-open backyard kitchen south)
    (door-between backyard living-room east)
    (door-open backyard living-room east)
    (door-between living-room backyard west)
    (door-open living-room backyard west)
    (door-between kitchen pantry south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry south)
    (door-between pantry kitchen north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen north)
    (door-between backyard driveway north)
    (door-closed backyard driveway north)
    (door-between driveway backyard south)
    (door-closed driveway backyard south)
  )
  (:goal
    (at driveway)
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))

You have already generated df and pf files according to the observations.
This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem exploration-step33)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen backyard living-room pantry driveway - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at backyard)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored backyard)
    (explored living-room)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen backyard north)
    (door-open kitchen backyard north)
    (door-between backyard kitchen south)
    (door-open backyard kitchen south)
    (door-between backyard living-room east)
    (door-open backyard living-room east)
    (door-between living-room backyard west)
    (door-open living-room backyard west)
    (door-between kitchen pantry south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry south)
    (door-between pantry kitchen north)
    (door-open pantry kitchen north)
    (door-between backyard driveway north)
    (door-closed backyard driveway north)
  )
  (:goal
    (and (not (explored driveway)))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)
